Here is the translation: And it came to me in a vision that I should accomplish this with the treatise, which is part of the work of hands, that is to say "surgery".
And because the work of hands is forgotten in our region and is estranged from everything everywhere, thus the knowledge is lost and decayed, and nothing remains of the powers except for small descriptions in books of the ancients that the hands have moved. And from this has come the error and vanity, and the intentions are closed and the knowledge is estranged.
It seems to me that I want to bring to life together the ordering of this treatise according to the way of exposition and declaration and abbreviation. and I will bring together the forms of the iron instruments of cautery, and other equipment of the work with the adjustment of the declaration and preparation of them, as it is necessary.
And for the reason that no good masters of hands are found in our time, it is the art of medicine extended. And it behoves him who undertakes to learn the science of anatomy, as Galien says, so that he knows the judgment of the limbs, and the forms and conjunctions and separations of the bones, and has knowledge of the bones and nerves and brains and the number of holes, and the movement and resting of the veins moving and resting, and the issue of their exit.
And for this reason said Hippocrates that the name is not much, and with the work is little; and similarly in the art of hand.
We say in the introduction of this book that whoever is not knowledgeable about the things mentioned beforehand, should beware so he does not fall into error and does not harm men.
Thus I have seen many of those who engage in this science, and then abandon it without knowledge and without experience.
Because I see a foolish doctor who treats an abscess of the womb or neck of a woman, and treats the arteries of the neck; for so much blood flows out that the woman falls dead in his hands.
And I see another doctor who treats a stone of a man's water, and the stone was large; he carried away with him a piece of the bladder, and the man died within three days.
And I had already been called by the doctor, and I saw the condition of the patient and the size of the stone, and if they had removed it well he would have died.
And I see another doctor who took in care the duke of our land who had a broken leg, and with the breakage he had a wound;
and the doctor, out of ignorance, held the breakage against the wound with a strong bandage, and did not leave the wound to heal itself, and thus he made it terminal;
and he commanded that it should not be untied at all;
and then he delayed so that his leg was completely swollen and his feet went to ruin.
I was called to come to him, and I hastened to come and release the leg; and when I dislocated it thus it was at peace and did not feel any pain.
But entirely the corruption was already confirmed in the member, and I could not heal it;
and the corruption did not cease to spread through the member so that the member was almost entirely lost.
And I saw another mirror that burst into an abscess, and then became inflamed due to the evil of its dominance.
For cancer, when it is pure of melancholic humor, it does not seem that one should touch it with iron unless it is in a place where one can completely remove what is corrupted.
And for this, dear sons, it is necessary that you know that the work of hands is divided into two sections: it is to know whether there is danger in many dispositions;
and I will show in each place of this book where there is fear and danger.
Because it is necessary that you beware, so that foolish mirrors cannot speak evil of you.
If you take your arms in custody, and undertake your maladies lightly and firmly, and use the best way so that by the grace of God you come to health and are praised.
and let the maladies expel the grievous sanities;
and remove your arms from that which makes you doubt, and have faith in yourselves so that you can come from this world to the other of glory.
Galen says among some of his warnings: Do not take a bad malady in hand, lest you be called foolish physician.

of other complications we have no less fear, especially in cold and moist diseases. And all the mirrors assemble and agree with the cautery.

The dislocation of the hand
The joint of the hand dislocates, and the return is easy, more than the other joints. However, it must be quickly returned to its place, in the same way that it was dislocated, so that the limb is not swollen, or an abscess forms there.
And the resetting is that you put the sick hand on a table, and stretch out the little fingers, and the doctor puts them even, so that he puts his palm on the appearance of the joint, and presses until it returns.
However, it is necessary that you check if it is well in its place; then put the sick hand with the palm of his hand on a table at extension and resetting. And if the dislocation is in the back of the hand, then place the patient's hand on the table, and the mirrors place their hand on the appearance of the joint.

And if he cannot move it well, and there is no swelling, then apply warm water, and rub it until it is healthy.

of the dislocation of the knee
The knee is dislocated in three ways: it is to know, inward, forward, and backward;

and put the plaster on, and make the leg adhere to the thigh, and bind them together strongly for three or four days, then release it;
and do not bother the patient to get up, until the limb is comforted.

of wound and of dislocation together
When a wound comes with a dislocation, and one wants to restore it, often the patient dies:
if you are not presumptuous in the cure, be wise in the art and do not have long experience, and be pitiful and merciful and slow, not harsh;
and use soothing remedies at the beginning of things for a hot abscess, and leave the patient in God's hands, if you do not see hope of health; and when you see hope, now reset the limb to its place, so that the hot abscess may leave;
and when the limb is in its place, administer soothing remedies for hot abscess, and treat the wound, as it requires, with dry ointments;
and if it is with dislocation to fracture, and often you will not be able to set them straight, even if you try to reduce the bone, do what we have said about simple illnesses;
and beware of entering into the way of fear, according to what I have said, for it is worth more according to your Creator, and for the safety of your arm and your body.
